ENTRY       EC 2.2.1.1                  Enzyme
NAME        transketolase;
            glycolaldehydetransferase
CLASS       Transferases;
            Transferring aldehyde or ketonic groups;
            Transketolases and transaldolases
SYSNAME     sedoheptulose-7-phosphate:D-glyceraldehyde-3-phosphate glycolaldehydetransferase
REACTION    sedoheptulose 7-phosphate + D-glyceraldehyde 3-phosphate = D-ribose 5-phosphate + D-xylulose 5-phosphate [RN:R01641]
ALL_REAC    R01641;
            (other) R01067 R01830 R06590 R06861 R06863
SUBSTRATE   sedoheptulose 7-phosphate [CPD:C05382];
            D-glyceraldehyde 3-phosphate [CPD:C00118]
PRODUCT     D-ribose 5-phosphate [CPD:C00117];
            D-xylulose 5-phosphate [CPD:C00231]
COMMENT     A thiamine-diphosphate protein. Wide specificity for both reactants, e.g. converts hydroxypyruvate and R-CHO into CO2 and R-CHOH-CO-CH2OH. The enzyme from the bacterium Alcaligenes faecalis shows high activity with D-erythrose 4-phosphate as acceptor.
HISTORY     EC 2.2.1.1 created 1961
REFERENCE   1  [PMID:14367398]
  AUTHORS   DE LA HABA G, LEDER IG, RACKER E.
  TITLE     Crystalline transketolase from bakers' yeast: isolation and properties.
  JOURNAL   J Biol Chem 214:409-26 (1955)
REFERENCE   2
  AUTHORS   Domagk, G.F. and Horecker, B.L.
  TITLE     Fructose and erythrose metabolism in Alcaligenes faecalis.
  JOURNAL   Arch Biochem Biophys 109:342-349 (1965)
REFERENCE   3  [PMID:13385248]

  JOURNAL   J Biol Chem 223:1009-19 (1956)
